Yet without fail pundits seem to blame the *activists* for.... Having opinions? Participating in politics?		If you think an institution's response to political pressure is bad you should blame the people in charge of that response.
Politics happens. Pressure comes from different groups for different reasons, and targets vary widely. What determines outcomes is how powerful decision-makers (university administrators and trustees, Fox and its advertisers) respond to political pressure.
The Tucker Carlson boycott is a good example of a situation like when students protest controversial speakers on college campuses where everyone gets confused about who actually has decisionmaking power. Political activists are not the relevant decision-makers in either case.
